<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r911143475">.mw-parser-output .module-shortcutboxplain{float:right;border:1px solid #aaa;background:#fff;margin:0 0 0 1em;padding:0.3em 0.6em 0.2em 0.6em;text-align:center;font-size:85%;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .module-shortcutlist{display:inline-block;border-bottom:1px solid #aaa;margin-bottom:0.2em;font-weight:normal}.mw-parser-output .module-shortcutanchordiv{position:relative;top:-3em}.mw-parser-output li .module-shortcutanchordiv{float:right}</style><div class="module-shortcutanchordiv"><span id="WP:CP"></span><span id="WP:COPYPROB"></span></div><div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note"><div class="module-shortcutlist"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcuts</a></div><ul><li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:CP&amp;redirect=no">WP:CP</a></span></li><li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:COPYPROB&amp;redirect=no">WP:COPYPROB</a></span></li></ul></div>
<p>This page is for listing and discussing <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Spotting_possible_copyright_violations" title="Wikipedia:Spotting possible copyright violations">possible copyright problems</a></b> involving <b>text</b> on Wikipedia, including pages which are suspected to be <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyright_violations" title="Wikipedia:Copyright violations">copyright violations</a></b>. Listings typically remain for at least five days before review and closure by a copyright problems clerk or administrator. During this time, interested contributors are invited to offer feedback about the problem at the relevant talk page, to propose revisions to the material, or to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requesting_copyright_permission" title="Wikipedia:Requesting copyright permission">request copyright permission</a>. After the listing period, a copyright problems board clerk or administrator will review the listing and take what further action may be necessary.
</p><p>Pages listed for copyright review appear in the bottom section of the page. The top includes information for people who have copyright concerns about pages or images, for those whose pages have been tagged for concerns, for community volunteers who'd like to help resolve concerns and for the clerks and administrators who volunteer here.
</p><p>To add a new listing, please go to <b><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/2020_February_27&amp;action=edit&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/preload">today's section</a></span></b>. Instructions for dealing with copyright concerns can be found at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyright_problems#Instructions_for_dealing_with_text-based_copyright_concerns" title="Wikipedia:Copyright problems">Instructions for dealing with text-based copyright concerns</a>.
</p>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">If you believe a Wikipedia page has infringed on your copyright, please see <a href="#Instructions">special note below</a>.<br />If a page you created has been marked as a copyright problem and you own copyright in the original publication (or have permission from the owner), please see <a href="#IOWN">this section</a>.</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Handling_previously_published_text_on_Wikipedia"><span id="Policy"></span>Handling previously published text on Wikipedia</span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copy-paste" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Copy-paste">Wikipedia:Copy-paste</a></div>
<p>Under the United States law that governs Wikipedia, <b>copyright is automatically assumed</b> as soon as any content (text or other media) is created in a <a href="/wiki/Tangible" class="mw-redirect" title="Tangible">physical</a> form. An author does not need to apply for or even claim copyright, for a copyright to exist. 
</p><p><i>Only</i> one of the following allows works to be reused in Wikimedia projects:  
</p><p>A) <b>Explicit Statement</b>.  An explicit statement (by the author, or by the holder of the rights to the work) that the material is either:
</p>
<ul><li>in the <a href="/wiki/Public_domain" title="Public domain">public domain</a>,</li>
<li>licensed with the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Text_of_Creative_Commons_Attribution-ShareAlike_3.0_Unported_License" title="Wikipedia:Text of Creative Commons Attribution-ShareAlike 3.0 Unported License">Creative Commons Attribution-Sharealike 3.0 Unported License</a> (CC-BY-SA), or</li>
<li>otherwise compatible with CC-BY-SA.</li></ul>
<p>B) <b>Public Domain</b>.  If the work is inherently in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Public_domain" title="Wikipedia:Public domain">public domain</a>, due to its age, source or lack of originality (such as <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Logos#Copyright-free_logos" title="Wikipedia:Logos">Copyright-free logos</a>); or
</p><p>C)  <b>Fair Use</b>.  United States law allows for <a href="/wiki/Fair_use" title="Fair use">fair use</a> of copyrighted content, and (within limits) Wikipedia does as well. Under <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Non-free_content" title="Wikipedia:Non-free content">guidelines for non-free content</a>, <i>brief</i> selections of copyrighted text may be used, but <i>only</i> if clearly marked and with full attribution. 
</p><p>Even if a source is public domain or compatibly licensed, material should be properly attributed in accordance with <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Plagiarism" title="Wikipedia:Plagiarism">Wikipedia:Plagiarism</a>. This is not only a matter of respecting local custom. When content is under a license that is compatible with Wikipedia's license, proper attribution may be <i>required</i>. If the terms of the compatible license are not met, use of the content can constitute a violation of copyright even <i>if</i> the license is compatible.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Repeated_copyright_violations">Repeated copyright violations</span></h3>
<p>Contributors who repeatedly post copyrighted material (text <i>or</i> images) may be subject to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CCI" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:CCI">contributor copyright investigations</a>, to help ensure the removal from the project of all copyrighted material posted in contravention of policy. Contributors who repeatedly post copyrighted material after appropriate warnings will be blocked from editing, to protect the project; see <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.law.cornell.edu/uscode/text/17/512">17 United States Code ยง 512</a>.
</p>
<h2><span id="Backwards_copying:_when_Wikipedia_had_.28or_may_have_had.29_it_first"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Backwards_copying:_when_Wikipedia_had_(or_may_have_had)_it_first"><span id="Backwards"></span>Backwards copying: when Wikipedia had (or may have had) it first</span></h2>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r911143475"/><div class="module-shortcutanchordiv"><span id="WP:BACKWARDSCOPY"></span></div><div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note"><div class="module-shortcutlist"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcut</a></div><ul><li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:BACKWARDSCOPY&amp;redirect=no">WP:BACKWARDSCOPY</a></span></li></ul></div>
<p>In some instances, it is clear that two pieces of text (one on Wikipedia, and one elsewhere) are copies of each other, but not clear which piece is the original and which is the copy. "Compliant" sites that copy Wikipedia text note that they have done so, but not all of our re-users are compliant. 
</p><p>If you've found such a case, you might first check the discussion page to see if a note has been added to the top of the talk page to allay people's concerns. If not, you can look for clues. Do other pages in the other website copy other Wikipedia articles? Did the content show up on Wikipedia all in once piece, placed by a single editor? If you don't see good evidence that Wikipedia had it first, it's a good idea to bring it up for investigation. You might follow the <a href="#Instructions">Instructions for listing</a> below or tag the article <code>{{<a href="/wiki/Template:Copy-paste" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Copy-paste">copy-paste</a>&#124;url=possible source}}</code> so that others can evaluate. 
</p><p>If you confirm definitely that the content was on Wikipedia first, please consider adding &#123;&#123;<a href="/wiki/Template:Backwardscopy" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Backwardscopy">backwardscopy</a>&#125;&#125; to the article's talk page with an explanation of how you know.
If you see an article somewhere else which was copied from Wikipedia without attribution, you might visit the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CC-BY-SA_Compliance" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:CC-BY-SA Compliance">CC-BY-SA compliance</a> page or <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Mirrors_and_forks" title="Wikipedia:Mirrors and forks">Wikipedia:Mirrors and forks</a>.
There are well documented cases of <a href="/wiki/Plagiarism_from_Wikipedia" title="Plagiarism from Wikipedia">plagiarism from Wikipedia</a> by external publications.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Instructions_for_dealing_with_text-based_copyright_concerns"><span id="Instructions"></span>Instructions for dealing with text-based copyright concerns</span></h2>
<p><span id="Instructions_for_listing_text-based_copyright_concerns"></span>
</p>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">"WP:CPI" redirects here. For the page that protects extremely high-risk templates, see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Cascade_protected_items" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Cascade protected items">Wikipedia:Cascade protected items</a>.</div>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r911143475"/><div class="module-shortcutanchordiv"><span id="WP:CPI"></span></div><div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note"><div class="module-shortcutlist"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcut</a></div><ul><li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:CPI&amp;redirect=no">WP:CPI</a></span></li></ul></div>
<div style="background-color: #fff0f0; border: 1px solid black; padding: 1ex; margin: 1ex; margin-right: 20em; min-width:20em"><b>Copyright owners</b>: If you believe Wikipedia is infringing <i>your</i> copyright, you may <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Request_for_immediate_removal_of_copyright_violation" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Request for immediate removal of copyright violation">request immediate removal</a> of the copyright violation by emailing us at <b><tt><span class="nowrap">info-en-c<img alt="@" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/At_sign.svg/15px-At_sign.svg.png" decoding="async" title="@" width="15" height="15" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/At_sign.svg/23px-At_sign.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/At_sign.svg/30px-At_sign.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="145" data-file-height="145" />wikimedia.org</span></tt></b>. Please provide the address or title of the page, and evidence to show that you are the legitimate copyright holder. Alternatively, you may contact Wikipedia's <a href="https://foundation.wikimedia.org/wiki/Designated_agent" class="extiw" title="wikimedia:Designated agent">designated agent</a> under the terms of the <a href="/wiki/Online_Copyright_Infringement_Liability_Limitation_Act" title="Online Copyright Infringement Liability Limitation Act">Online Copyright Infringement Liability Limitation Act</a>. You are also welcome to follow the procedures here. See <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:C#Owner" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:C">the copyright policy for more information.</a></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Blatant_infringement">Blatant infringement</span></h3>
<p>Pages exhibiting blatant copyright infringements may be <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Speedy_deletions" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Speedy deletions">speedily deleted</a> if:
</p>
<ul><li>Content was copied from a source which does not have a license compatible with Wikipedia, and the content was copied from that source to Wikipedia and not the other way around (Wikipedia has <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:FORK" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:FORK">numerous mirrors</a>);</li>
<li>The page can neither be restored to a previous revision without infringing content, nor would the page be viable if the infringing content were removed.</li>
<li>There is no credible assertion of public domain, fair use, or a free license.</li></ul>
<div style="border: 1px solid black; padding: 1ex; margin: 1ex; margin-right: 20em; min-width:20em">
<p>To nominate an article for speedy deletion for copyright concerns, add one of these to the page:
</p>
<dl><dd><dl><dd><ul><li><code>{{<a href="/wiki/Template:Db-copyvio" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Db-copyvio">db-copyvio</a>&#124;url=<i>insert URL of source here</i>}}</code></li>
<li><code>{{<a href="/wiki/Template:Db-copyvio" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Db-copyvio">db-copyvio</a>&#124;<i>describe non-web source here</i>}}</code></li></ul></dd></dl></dd></dl>
<p>Both of these templates will generate a notice that you should give the contributor of the content. This is important to help ensure that they do not <i>continue</i> to add copyrighted content to Wikipedia.  An <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Administrators" title="Wikipedia:Administrators">administrator</a> will examine the article and decide whether to delete it or not. You should <b>not</b> blank the page in this instance.
</p>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Suspected_or_complicated_infringement">Suspected or complicated infringement</span></h3>
<p>If infringement is not blatant or the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CSD#G12" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:CSD">speedy deletion criteria</a> do not apply:
</p>
<ul><li>Remove or rewrite the infringing text avoiding <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:COPYVIO" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:COPYVIO">violations of copyright</a> or <a href="/wiki/Help:Reverting" title="Help:Reverting">revert</a> the page to a non-copyrighted version if you can.
<dl><dd><span id="textremains"></span>The infringing text will remain in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Page_history" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Page history">page history</a> for archival reasons (allowing evaluation by non-administrative editors) unless the copyright holder asks the <a href="/wiki/Wikimedia_Foundation" title="Wikimedia Foundation">Wikimedia Foundation</a> to remove it. After determination that it is a copyvio, it should be tagged for &#123;&#123;<a href="/wiki/Template:Copyvio-revdel" title="Template:Copyvio-revdel">copyvio-revdel</a>&#125;&#125;. Please note the reason for removal in the <a href="/wiki/Help:Edit_summary" title="Help:Edit summary">edit summary</a> and at the article's talk page (you may wish to use &#123;{<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Substitution" title="Wikipedia:Substitution">subst</a>:<a href="/wiki/Template:Cclean" title="Template:Cclean">cclean</a>}}). When possible, please identify and alert the contributor of the material to the problem. The template &#123;&#123;<a href="/wiki/Template:Uw-copyright" title="Template:Uw-copyright">Uw-copyright</a>&#125;&#125; may be used for this purpose.</dd></dl></li>
<li>However, if all revisions have copyright problems, the removal of the copyright problem is contested, or reversion/removal is otherwise complicated:</li></ul>
<div style="border: 1px solid black; padding: 1ex; margin: 1ex; margin-right: 20em; min-width:20em">
<ul><li><b>Replace</b> the text with one of the following:<blockquote><p><code>{{<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Substitution" title="Wikipedia:Substitution">subst</a>:<a href="/wiki/Template:Copyvio" title="Template:Copyvio">copyvio</a>&#124;url=<i>insert URL here</i>}}</code><code>{{<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Substitution" title="Wikipedia:Substitution">subst</a>:<a href="/wiki/Template:Copyvio" title="Template:Copyvio">copyvio</a>&#124;<i>identify non-web source here</i>}}</code></p></blockquote></li>
<li>Go to <b><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/2020_February_27&amp;action=edit">today's section</a></b> and add <blockquote><p><code>* <span style="white-space:nowrap;">&#123;&#123;subst:article-cv&#124;<i>PageName</i>&#125;&#125;</span> from [<i>insert URL or identify non-web source here</i>] ~~~~</code></p></blockquote> to the bottom of the list. Put the page's name in place of <i>"PageName"</i>. If you do not have a URL, enter a description of the source. (This text can be copied from the top of the template after substituting it and the page name and url will be filled for you.) If there is not already a page for the day, as yours would be the first listing, please add a header to the top of the page using the page for another date as an example.</li>
<li>Advise the contributor of the material at their talk page. The template on the now blanked page supplies a notice you may use for that purpose.</li></ul>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Instructions_for_special_cases">Instructions for special cases</span></h3>
<ul><li><b>Probable copyvios without a known source</b>: If you suspect that a page contains a copyright violation, but you cannot find a source for the violation (so you can't be sure that it's a violation), do not list it here. Instead, place {{cv-unsure|~~~|2=FULL_URL}} on the page's talk page, but replace FULL_URL with the full URL of the page version that you believe contains a violation. (To determine the URL, click on "Permanent link" in the toolbox area, and copy the URL.)</li>
<li><b>Instances where one contributor has verifiably introduced copyright problems into multiple pages or files</b> and assistance is needed in further review: See <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Contributor_copyright_investigations" title="Wikipedia:Contributor copyright investigations">Wikipedia:Contributor copyright investigations</a>.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Instructions_for_handling_image_copyright_concerns"><span id="Images"></span>Instructions for handling image copyright concerns</span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Guide_to_image_deletion" title="Wikipedia:Guide to image deletion">Wikipedia:Guide to image deletion</a></div>
<p>Image copyright concerns are not handled on this board. For images that are clear copyright violations, follow the procedure for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CSD#I9" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:CSD">speedy deletion</a>; otherwise list at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Files_for_discussion" title="Wikipedia:Files for discussion">Files for Discussion</a>. To request assistance with contributors who have infringed copyright in multiple articles or files, see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Contributor_copyright_investigations" title="Wikipedia:Contributor copyright investigations">Wikipedia:Contributor copyright investigations</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Responding_to_articles_listed_for_copyright_investigation"><span id="Responding"></span>Responding to articles listed for copyright investigation</span></h2>
<div style="background-color: #fff0f0; border: 1px solid black; padding: 1ex; margin: 1ex; margin-right: 20em; min-width:20em"><center>
<i>Copyright owners and people editing on their behalf or with their permission, please see <a href="#IOWN">below</a>.</i></center>
</div>
<p>Any contributor is welcome to help investigate articles listed for copyright concerns, although only administrators, copyright problems board clerks, and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:OTRS" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:OTRS">OTRS</a> team members should remove &#123;&#123;<a href="/wiki/Template:Copyvio" title="Template:Copyvio">copyvio</a>&#125;&#125; tags and mark listings resolved. 
</p><p>Assistance might include supplying evidence of non-infringement (or, conversely, of infringement) or obtaining and verifying permission of license. You might also help by rewriting problematic articles.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Supplying_evidence_of_non-infringement">Supplying evidence of non-infringement</span></h3>
<p>Articles are listed for copyright investigation because contributors have reason to suspect they constitute a copyright concern, but not every article listed here is actually a copyright problem. Sometimes, the content was <a href="#Backwards">on Wikipedia first</a>. Sometimes, the article is <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Public_domain" title="Wikipedia:Public domain">public domain</a> or <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:COMPLIC" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:COMPLIC">compatibly licensed</a> and can be easily fixed by supplying attribution (e.g. through a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:DUMMY" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:DUMMY">dummy edit</a>). Sometimes, the person who placed it here <i>is</i> the copyright owner of freely-licensed material and this simply needs to be verified.
</p><p>If you can provide information to prove license or public domain status of the article, please do. It doesn't matter if you do it under the listing for the article on the copyright problems board or on the talk page of the article; a link or a clear explanation can be very helpful when a clerk or administrator evaluates the matter. (As listings are not immediately addressed on the board, it may take a few days after you make your note before a response is provided.)
</p><p>If the article is tagged for &#123;&#123;<a href="/wiki/Template:Copyvio" title="Template:Copyvio">copyvio</a>&#125;&#125;, you should allow an administrator or copyright problems clerk to remove the tag. If the article is tagged for &#123;&#123;<a href="/wiki/Template:Copy-paste" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Copy-paste">copy-paste</a>&#125;&#125; or &#123;&#123;<a href="/wiki/Template:Close_paraphrasing" title="Template:Close paraphrasing">close paraphrasing</a>&#125;&#125;, you may remove the tag from the article when the problem is addressed (or disproven), but please do not close the listing on the copyright problems board itself.
</p>
<h3><span id="Obtaining.2Fverifying_permission"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Obtaining/verifying_permission">Obtaining/verifying permission</span></h3>
<p>Sometimes material was placed on Wikipedia with the permission of the copyright owner. Sometimes copyright owners are willing to give permission (and proper license!) even if it was not. 
</p><p>Any contributor can write to the owner of copyright and check whether they gave or will give permission (or maybe they in fact posted it here!). See <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Example_requests_for_permission" title="Wikipedia:Example requests for permission">Wikipedia:Example requests for permission</a>. In either case, unless a statement authorizing the material under compatible license is placed online at the point of original publication, permission will need to be confirmed through e-mail to the Wikimedia Foundation. See <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Confirmation_of_permission" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Confirmation of permission">Wikipedia:Confirmation of permission</a>. If a compatible license is placed online at the point of original publication, please provide a link to that under the listing for the article on the copyright problems board or on the talk page of the article.
</p><p>Please note that it may take a few days for letters to clear once they are sent. Do not worry if the content is deleted prematurely; it can be restored at any point usable permission is logged.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rewriting_content">Rewriting content</span></h3>
<p>Any contributor may rewrite articles that are or seem to be copyight problems to exclude duplicated or closely paraphrased text. When articles or sections of articles are blanked as copyright problems, this is done on a temporary page at <i>Talk:PAGENAME/Temp</i> so that the new material can be copied over the old. (The template blanking the article will link to the specific temporary page.) 
</p><p>Please do not copy over the version of the article that is a copyright problem as your base. All copied content, or material derived from it, should be removed first. Other content from the article can be used, if there is no reason to believe that it may be a copyright issue as well. It is often a good idea - and essential when the content is copied from an inaccessible source such as a book - to locate the point where the material entered the article and eliminate all text added by that contributor. This will help avoid inadvertently continuing the copyright issues in your rewrite. <i>If you use any text at all from the earlier version of the article, please leave a note at the talk page of the article to alert the administrator or clerk who addresses the listing</i>. The history of the old article will then have to be retained. (If the original turns out to be non-infringing, the two versions of the article can be merged.) 
</p><p>Rewrites can be done directly in articles that have been tagged for &#123;&#123;<a href="/wiki/Template:Close_paraphrasing" title="Template:Close paraphrasing">close paraphrasing</a>&#125;&#125; and &#123;&#123;<a href="/wiki/Template:Copy-paste" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Copy-paste">copy-paste</a>&#125;&#125;, with those tags removed after the rewrite is complete.
</p><p>Please review <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copy-paste" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Copy-paste">Wikipedia:Copy-paste</a> and the linked guidelines and policies within it if necessary to review Wikipedia's practices for handling non-free text. Reviewing <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Plagiarism" title="Wikipedia:Plagiarism">Wikipedia:Plagiarism</a> is also helpful, particularly where content is compatibly licensed or public domain. Repairing these issues can sometimes be as simple as supplying proper attribution.
</p>
<h3><span id="Copyright_owners_who_submitted_their_own_work_to_Wikipedia_.28or_people_editing_on_their_behalf.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Copyright_owners_who_submitted_their_own_work_to_Wikipedia_(or_people_editing_on_their_behalf)"><span id="IOWN"></span>Copyright owners who submitted their own work to Wikipedia (or people editing on their behalf)</span></h3>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r911143475"/><div class="module-shortcutanchordiv"><span id="WP:IOWN"></span></div><div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note"><div class="module-shortcutlist"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Policy shortcut</a></div><ul><li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:IOWN&amp;redirect=no">WP:IOWN</a></span></li></ul></div>
<p>If you submitted work to Wikipedia which you had previously published and your submission was marked as a potential infringement of copyright, then stating on the article's talk page that you are the copyright holder of the work (or acting as his or her agent), while not likely to prevent deletion, helps. To completely resolve copyright concerns, it is sufficient to either:
</p>
<ul><li>Link to a note permitting reuse under the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Text_of_Creative_Commons_Attribution-ShareAlike_3.0_Unported_License" title="Wikipedia:Text of Creative Commons Attribution-ShareAlike 3.0 Unported License">Creative Commons Attribution-Sharealike 3.0 Unported License</a> (CC-BY-SA) and the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Text_of_the_GNU_Free_Documentation_License" title="Wikipedia:Text of the GNU Free Documentation License">GNU Free Documentation License</a> (GFDL) (unversioned, with no invariant sections, front-cover texts, or back-cover texts) at the site of the original publication; or</li>
<li>Send an email from an address associated with the original publication to <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="mailto:permissions-commons@wikimedia.org">permissions-commons@wikimedia.org</a> or a postal message to the <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://wikimediafoundation.org/wiki/Contact_us">Wikimedia Foundation</a>, ideally using the email template at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CONSENT" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:CONSENT">WP:CONSENT</a>.</li></ul>
<p>See also <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Donating_copyrighted_materials" title="Wikipedia:Donating copyrighted materials">Wikipedia:Donating copyrighted materials</a>.
</p><p>Please note that it may take a bit of time for letters and e-mails to clear once they are sent. Do not worry if the content is deleted prematurely; it can be restored at any point usable permission is logged. Your e-mail will receive a response whether the permission is usable or not. If you have not received a response to your letter within two weeks, it is a good idea to follow up.
</p><p>One other factor you should consider, however, is that content that has been previously published elsewhere <i>may</i> not meet Wikipedia's specific guidelines and policies. If you are not familiar with these policies and guidelines, please review especially <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Five_pillars" title="Wikipedia:Five pillars">the core policies</a> that govern the project. This may help prepare you to deal with any other issues with the text that may arise.
</p><p>Should you choose to rewrite the content rather than release it under the requisite license, please see <a href="#Rewriting_content">above</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Information_about_the_people_who_process_copyright_problems_listed_on_the_board">Information about the people who process copyright problems listed on the board</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Copyright_problems_board_clerks"><span id="Clerks"></span>Copyright problems board clerks</span></h3>
<p><i>For a more complete description of clerks and their duties, as well as a list of active clerks, please see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/Clerks" title="Wikipedia:Copyright problems/Clerks">Wikipedia:Copyright problems/Clerks</a>.</i>
</p><p>Copyright problems board clerks are experienced editors on Wikipedia who have demonstrated familiarity with Wikipedia's approach to non-free text and its processes for dealing with them. They are trusted to evaluate and close listings, although their closures may sometimes require completion by administrators, when use of administrative tools is required. Clerks are periodically reviewed by the administrators who work in copyright areas on Wikipedia.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Copyright_problems_board_administrators"><span id="Admins"></span>Copyright problems board administrators</span></h3>
<p><i>For a more complete description of administrators on Wikipedia, please see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Administrators" title="Wikipedia:Administrators">Wikipedia:Administrators</a>.</i>
</p><p>Any administrator may work the copyright problems board. Working the copyright problems board may involve evaluating listings personally or using tools as necessary to complete closures by clerks. Clerks have been evaluated in their work, and their recommendations may be implemented without double-checking, although any administrator is welcome to review recommendations and discuss them with the clerks in question.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Closing_listings"><span id="Advice"></span>Closing listings</span></h2>
<p>Pages should stay listed for a minimum of <b>5 days</b> before they are checked and processed by copyright problems board clerks, <b>7 days</b> before they are checked or processed by administrators, who close the daily listings. OTRS agents who verify images may close listings at any time.
</p><p>For advice for resolving listings, see:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/Advice_for_admins" title="Wikipedia:Copyright problems/Advice for admins">Wikipedia:Copyright problems/Advice for admins</a> (OTRS agents, see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/Advice_for_admins#Checking_for_permission" title="Wikipedia:Copyright problems/Advice for admins">section there</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/Clerks#Advice_for_clerks" title="Wikipedia:Copyright problems/Clerks">Wikipedia:Copyright problems/Clerks#Advice for clerks</a></li></ul>
<p>The templates collected at <a href="/wiki/Template:CPC" title="Template:CPC">Template:CPC</a> may be useful for administrators, clerks and OTRS agents noting resolution.
</p>

</p>

<ul><li><span id="Meanings_of_minor_planet_names:_100001โ101000"></span><a href="/wiki/Meanings_of_minor_planet_names:_100001%E2%80%93101000" title="Meanings of minor planet names: 100001โ101000">Meanings of minor planet names: 100001โ101000</a> <span class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Meanings_of_minor_planet_names:_100001%E2%80%93101000&amp;action=history">history</a> ยท <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Meanings_of_minor_planet_names:_100001%E2%80%93101000&amp;diff=0">last edit</a> ยท <a href="/w/index.php?title=Talk:Meanings_of_minor_planet_names:_100001%E2%80%93101000/Temp&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Talk:Meanings of minor planet names: 100001โ101000/Temp (page does not exist)">rewrite</a>)</span> from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://ssd.jpl.nasa.gov/sbdb.cgi?sstr=100007#content">Jet Propulsion Laboratory</a></li></ul>
<dl><dd>We have over 400 pages of <a href="/wiki/Meanings_of_minor_planet_names" title="Meanings of minor planet names">Meanings of minor planet names</a> that may have the same issue, so I picked the 100001โ101000 example at random. For most of the entries, the description in the <i>This minor planet was named for...</i> column was copied or very closely paraphrased from the "JPL" source linked in the <i>Ref ยท Catalog</i> column. This was previously discussed at a tangentially related <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/List_of_minor_planets:_500001%E2%80%93501000" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/List of minor planets: 500001โ501000">AfD</a> where some editors felt it was a copyright violation while others argued that the data was "freely available from NASA" and not subject to copyright. JPL's copyright statements <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://ssd.jpl.nasa.gov/?faq#A05">[5]</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.jpl.nasa.gov/privacy/web/">[6]</a> may be of use. โ<a href="/wiki/User:Dlthewave" title="User:Dlthewave">dlthewave</a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Dlthewave" title="User talk:Dlthewave">โ</a> 21:36, 1 July 2019 (UTC)
<dl><dd>Simple phrases such as "This minor planet was named for &lt;name&gt;" cannot be copyrighted. I don't know how many entries fall outside this "simple" phrasing, but it's something to consider. <a href="/wiki/User:Primefac" title="User:Primefac">Primefac</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Primefac" title="User talk:Primefac">talk</a>) 19:40, 7 July 2019 (UTC)</dd></dl></dd></dl>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="21_November_2019"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/2019_November_21" title="Wikipedia:Copyright problems/2019 November 21">21 November 2019</a></span></h4>
<p>I have found three instances of extensive cut-and-paste by <a href="/wiki/User:Dhollm" title="User:Dhollm">Dhollm</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Dhollm" title="User talk:Dhollm">talk</a>&#160;<b>ยท</b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Dhollm" title="Special:Contributions/Dhollm">contribs</a>), and am concerned that their work dating years may be copyvio.  I do not have time to continue looking, but suggest that a copyright investigation may need to be opened to check every edit from this editor.
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/Harlem_River" title="Harlem River">Harlem River</a> (created in 2010, acknowledging text from gsapp.org,<a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?diff=374372566">[13]</a>, a site which was webarchived in 2011 <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20110726133540/http://www.gsapp.org/Archive/HP/2003-2004/history.html">[14]</a>).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pineywoods_cattle" title="Pineywoods cattle">Pineywoods cattle</a> since its creation (much of the article was mirrored later, but some of the article was taken from the same org that later mirrored Wikipedia); not sure what revdel may be needed because of the mix.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Electrostatic_fluid_accelerator" title="Electrostatic fluid accelerator">Electrostatic fluid accelerator</a> was moved from draft space with what looks like it might be cut-and-paste from a journal article, with citations filled in later with other edits.<a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Electrostatic_fluid_accelerator&amp;oldid=380141069">[15]</a>  Access to books and journals needed, but <b>citations</b> from the article infringed at Harlem River, and acknowledged in edit summary, were copied in verbatim as in this instance. (According to responses on Dhollm's talk page, these may be student papers that do not have copyright releases. <a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=User_talk:Dhollm&amp;oldid=869688321#Copyright?">[16]</a>  Independently, reliability is not established if they are student papers.)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Convection" title="Convection">Convection</a> <a class="external free" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?diff=379862963">https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?diff=379862963</a> should be checked as well, versus journals, if warranted based on what is found elsewhere.</li></ol>
<p><a href="/wiki/User:SandyGeorgia" title="User:SandyGeorgia"><b>Sandy</b><span style="color: green;">Georgia</span></a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:SandyGeorgia" title="User talk:SandyGeorgia">Talk</a>)  02:05, 21 November 2019 (UTC)
</p><p>Hi, does this fall under copyright violation? <a href="/wiki/European_Association_for_Artificial_Intelligence#Fellowship" title="European Association for Artificial Intelligence">European Association for Artificial Intelligence#Fellowship</a>, [<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.eurai.org/apply_for/fellow_program">[17]</a>] <a href="/wiki/User:ZaaraTE" title="User:ZaaraTE">ZaaraTE</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:ZaaraTE" title="User talk:ZaaraTE">talk</a>) 15:21, 21 November 2019 (UTC)
</p>
<ul><li>While reviewing this draft, I found that many parts of the draft appear to be copied from <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://issuu.com/sojiadesugba/docs/prof__60_mag_spread">https://issuu.com/sojiadesugba/docs/prof__60_mag_spread</a>. Please see <a class="external free" href="https://tools.wmflabs.org/copyvios/?lang=en&amp;project=wikipedia&amp;oldid=924352304&amp;action=compare&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.accibestcentre.com%2Fprofessor-adesugba%2F">https://tools.wmflabs.org/copyvios/?lang=en&amp;project=wikipedia&amp;oldid=924352304&amp;action=compare&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.accibestcentre.com%2Fprofessor-adesugba%2F</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Taewangkorea" title="User:Taewangkorea">Taewangkorea</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Taewangkorea" title="User talk:Taewangkorea">talk</a>) 17:58, 21 November 2019 (UTC)</li></ul>

However, the text is not in conformance with Wikipedia style guidelines (in particular it's not in encyclopedic style), so I suspect it's copied from an earlier source, perhaps a paper that covered much of the same ground as the book. Since Wikipedia may be the original source, I have not removed the text. <a href="/wiki/User:Hairy_Dude" title="User:Hairy Dude">Hairy Dude</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Hairy_Dude" title="User talk:Hairy Dude">talk</a>) 00:33, 20 January 2020 (UTC)

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="New_listings">New listings</span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Some issues may not be displayed on this page due to template transclusion limits. This can be alleviated by clearing the backlog.</div>
<p><b>New listings are not added directly to this page but are instead on daily reports.</b> To add a new listing, please go to <b><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/2020_February_27&amp;action=edit&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/preload">today's section</a></span></b>. Instructions for adding new listings can be found at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyright_problems#Instructions_for_listing_text-based_copyright_concerns" title="Wikipedia:Copyright problems">Instructions for listing text-based copyright concerns</a>. Entries may not be reviewed and are not closed for <i>at least</i> 7 days to give the original authors of the article time to deal with the problem.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Older_than_5_days">Older than 5 days</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Below are articles that have been listed here for longer than 5 days. At this point, they may be processed by a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/Clerks" title="Wikipedia:Copyright problems/Clerks">copyright problems board clerk</a>. After 7 days, they may be closed by an administrator.</div>

</p>

<ul><li><span id="Draft:Old_Scotch_Collegians_Football_Club"></span><a href="/wiki/Draft:Old_Scotch_Collegians_Football_Club" title="Draft:Old Scotch Collegians Football Club">Draft:Old Scotch Collegians Football Club</a> <span class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Draft:Old_Scotch_Collegians_Football_Club&amp;action=history">history</a> ยท <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Draft:Old_Scotch_Collegians_Football_Club&amp;diff=0">last edit</a> ยท <a href="/w/index.php?title=Draft_talk:Old_Scotch_Collegians_Football_Club/Temp&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Draft talk:Old Scotch Collegians Football Club/Temp (page does not exist)">rewrite</a>)</span> from <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.oscfc.com.au/club-history.html">[29]</a> <a href="/wiki/User:Cthomas3" title="User:Cthomas3"><i><b><span style="font-family: Courier New; font-size: larger; color: black;"><span style="color: brown;">C</span>Thomas<sup style="font-size: x-small; color: brown;">3</sup></span></b></i></a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Cthomas3" title="User talk:Cthomas3">talk</a>) 05:12, 24 February 2020 (UTC)</li></ul>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="26_February_2020"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/2020_February_26" title="Wikipedia:Copyright problems/2020 February 26">26 February 2020</a></span></h4>
<ul><li><span id="HIV/AIDS_in_China"></span><a href="/wiki/HIV/AIDS_in_China" title="HIV/AIDS in China">HIV/AIDS in China</a> <span class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=HIV/AIDS_in_China&amp;action=history">history</a> ยท <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=HIV/AIDS_in_China&amp;diff=0">last edit</a> ยท <a href="/w/index.php?title=Talk:HIV/AIDS_in_China/Temp&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Talk:HIV/AIDS in China/Temp (page does not exist)">rewrite</a>)</span> Article plagiarized from at least three identifiable academic journal articles, as detailed at <a href="/wiki/Talk:HIV/AIDS_in_China#Deletion_of_Massive_Plagiarism" title="Talk:HIV/AIDS in China">Talk:HIV/AIDS in China#Deletion of Massive Plagiarism</a>. Last identifiable un-plagiarized version is from 2007, rollback needed? <a href="/wiki/User:WhinyTheYounger" title="User:WhinyTheYounger">WhinyTheYounger</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:WhinyTheYounger" title="User talk:WhinyTheYounger">talk</a>) 05:47, 26 February 2020 (UTC)</li>
<li><span id="Draft:Shlomit_Yanisky-Ravid"></span><a href="/wiki/Draft:Shlomit_Yanisky-Ravid" title="Draft:Shlomit Yanisky-Ravid">Draft:Shlomit Yanisky-Ravid</a> <span class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Draft:Shlomit_Yanisky-Ravid&amp;action=history">history</a> ยท <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Draft:Shlomit_Yanisky-Ravid&amp;diff=0">last edit</a> ยท <a href="/w/index.php?title=Draft_talk:Shlomit_Yanisky-Ravid/Temp&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Draft talk:Shlomit Yanisky-Ravid/Temp (page does not exist)">rewrite</a>)</span> from <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://www.fordham.edu/info/23193/school_of_law_visiting_faculty/11170/shlomit_yanisky-ravid">https://www.fordham.edu/info/23193/school_of_law_visiting_faculty/11170/shlomit_yanisky-ravid</a>. Foundational. G12 has been declined, but I don't think copying at this level can be considered remotely acceptable. <a href="/wiki/User:Justlettersandnumbers" title="User:Justlettersandnumbers">Justlettersandnumbers</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Justlettersandnumbers" title="User talk:Justlettersandnumbers">talk</a>) 16:26, 26 February 2020 (UTC)</li>
<li><span id="List_of_Zoboomafoo_episodes"></span><a href="/wiki/List_of_Zoboomafoo_episodes" title="List of Zoboomafoo episodes">List of Zoboomafoo episodes</a> <span class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_Zoboomafoo_episodes&amp;action=history">history</a> ยท <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_Zoboomafoo_episodes&amp;diff=0">last edit</a> ยท <a href="/w/index.php?title=Talk:List_of_Zoboomafoo_episodes/Temp&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Talk:List of Zoboomafoo episodes/Temp (page does not exist)">rewrite</a>)</span> from <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://www.kqed.org/tv/programs/archive/index.jsp?pgmid=8183&amp;date=20050901">https://www.kqed.org/tv/programs/archive/index.jsp?pgmid=8183&amp;date=20050901</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Ttwaring" title="User:Ttwaring">Ttwaring</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ttwaring" title="User talk:Ttwaring">talk</a>) 21:55, 26 February 2020 (UTC)</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="27_February_2020"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyright_problems/2020_February_27" title="Wikipedia:Copyright problems/2020 February 27">27 February 2020</a></span></h4>
<ul><li><ul><li><span id="Phi_Epsilon_Kappa"></span><a href="/wiki/Phi_Epsilon_Kappa" title="Phi Epsilon Kappa">Phi Epsilon Kappa</a> <span class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Phi_Epsilon_Kappa&amp;action=history">history</a> ยท <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Phi_Epsilon_Kappa&amp;diff=0">last edit</a> ยท <a href="/w/index.php?title=Talk:Phi_Epsilon_Kappa/Temp&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Talk:Phi Epsilon Kappa/Temp (page does not exist)">rewrite</a>)</span> Large addition to <a href="/wiki/Phi_Epsilon_Kappa" title="Phi Epsilon Kappa">Phi Epsilon Kappa</a>, but turned out to be largely copied from pages at <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://www.phiepsilonkappa.org/">https://www.phiepsilonkappa.org/</a> added description from <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://www.phiepsilonkappa.org/">https://www.phiepsilonkappa.org/</a> , chapter list (which as a list probably isn't a problem from <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://www.phiepsilonkappa.org/chapters">https://www.phiepsilonkappa.org/chapters</a> and most seriously the history from <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://www.phiepsilonkappa.org/about-us">https://www.phiepsilonkappa.org/about-us</a> . I don't think I'd have any problem with a rewrite, but would like advice. <a href="/wiki/User:Naraht" title="User:Naraht">Naraht</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Naraht" title="User talk:Naraht">talk</a>) 11:37, 27 February 2020 (UTC)</li></ul></li></ul>
